*recv_buffer += kAtomStride;\n59\t        }\n60\t    }\n61\t};\n62\t\n63\t// Int4 symmetric quantization codec.\n64\t// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Int4 in blocks of 4 *\n65\t// kThreadGroupSize.\n66\ttemplate <typename T, int world_size>\n67\tstruct CodecQ4 : public CodecBase\n68\t{\n69\t    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n70\t\n71\t    // Codec tile size __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ4(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n104\t\n105\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n106\t                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n107\t    {\n108\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n109\t        {\n110\t            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n111\t\n112\t            // Compute the absolute maximum of the atom in the thread group\n113\t            // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n114\t            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n115\t\n116\t            // Derive scales\n117\t            int decoding_scale;\n118\t            int encoding_scale;\n119\t            decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n120\t            encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n121\t            encoding_scale = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n122\t\n123\t            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n124\t            int32x4_t w;\n125\t            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n126\t            {\n127\t                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], i++)\n141\t                {\n142\t                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n143\t                }\n144\t            }\n145\t\n146\t            // Pack 8 x q4 into stores the scale\n151\t            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n152\t            int32_t* qw_ptr   = reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n153\t            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n154\t\n155\t            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n156\t            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n157\t            {\n158\t                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n159\t            }\n160\t        }\n161\t    }\n162\t\n163\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n164\t                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n165\t    {\n166\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n167\t        {\n168\t            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n169\t            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n170\t            int32_t* qw_ptr   = reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n171\t            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n172\t\n173\t            int32_t qw = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qw_ptr);\n174\t            int qs     = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n175\t\n176\t            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n177\t\n178\t            // Unpack q4 into f16x8_t\n179\t            int32x4_t w;\n180\t            {\n181\t                static constexpr uint kMask000F   = 0x000F000F;\n182\t                static constexpr uint kHalf2_1024 = 0x64006400; // {1024.0, 1024.0}, fp16x2_t\n183\t                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1032 = 0xE408E408; // {-1032.0, -1032.0}, fp16x2_t\n184\t\n185\t                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n186\t                {\n187\t                    if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n188\t                    {\n189\t                        int32_t q4 = ((qw >> (i * 4)) & kMask000F) | kHalf2_1024;\n190\t                        w[i]       = packed_add<half>(q4, kHalf2_1032);\n191\t                    }\n192\t                    else\n193\t                    {\n194\t                        int32_t int16_2        = (qw >> (i * 4)) & kMask000F;\n195\t                        int16_t low            = static_cast<int16_t>(int16_2 & 0xFFFF);\n196\t                        int16_t high           = static_cast<int16_t>((int16_2 >> 16) & 0xFFFF);\n197\t                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n198\t                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n199\t                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n200\t                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n201\t                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n202\t                    }\n203\t                }\n204\t            }\n205\t\n206\t            // Apply decoding scales\n207\t            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n208\t            {\n209\t                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n210\t            }\n211\t\n212\t            data[k] = w;\n213\t        }\n214\t    }\n215\t};\n216\t\n217\t// Int3 symmetric quantization codec.\n218\t// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Int3 in blocks of 4 *\n219\t// kThreadGroupSize. Uniform symmetric quantization (round-to-int + clip),\n220\t// matching the structure of CodecQ4. Signed range is [-4, +3].\n221\ttemplate <typename T, int world_size>\n222\tstruct CodecQ3 : public CodecBase\n223\t{\n224\t    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n225\t\n226\t    // Layout per quantization block (32 values = 8 threads * 4 fp16x2 lanes):\n227\t    //  - each thread owns 8 values and writes:\n228\t    //      * q2 payload : 8 * 2 bits -> uint16 (2 bytes)\n229\t    //      * q1 payload : 8 * 1 bit  -> uint8  (1 byte)\n230\t    //  - one scale is shared per 32 values and written by group leader.\n231\t    //\n232\t    // kRankTileStride is split as:\n233\t    //   [0   .. 511] : q2 payload region (256 threads * 2 bytes)\n234\t    //   [512 .. 767] : q1 payload region (256 threads * 1 byte)\n235\t    //   [768 .. 895] : scale region (32 groups * 4 bytes)\n236\t    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n237\t    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 896;\n238\t    static constexpr int kRankTileQ1Offset        = 512;\n239\t    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 768;\n240\t    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n241\t    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n242\t                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n243\t\n244\t    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n245\t\n246\t    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n247\t    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n248\t\n249\t    // {-1/4.0h, -1/4.0h}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t. Sign-flipped so absmax maps\n250\t    // to -4; the sign cancels with decoding_scale on the recv side.\n251\t    static constexpr int kScaleFactor = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xB400B400 : 0xBE80BE80;\n252\t\n253\t    // {1e-7, 1e-7}, f16x2_t\n254\t    static constexpr int kScaleEpsilon = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7;\n255\t\n256\t    // {-4, -4}, f16x2_t / std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x42004200 : 0x40404040;\n261\t\n262\t    // {+4, +4}, int16x2_t -- shifts signed [-4, +3] to unsigned [0, 7].\n263\t    static constexpr int kRangeBias = 0x00040004;\n264\t\n265\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ3(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n266\t\n267\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n268\t                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n269\t    {\n270\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n271\t        {\n272\t            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n273\t\n274\t            // 1) Per-group dynamic scale (shared across 32 values).\n275\t            int wblockmax      = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n276\t            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n277\t            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n278\t            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n279\t\n280\t            // 2) Scale + clip to signed int3 range [-4, +3].\n281\t            int32x4_t w;\n282\t            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n283\t            {\n284\t                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n285\t                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n286\t                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n287\t            }\n288\t\n289\t            // 3) Round to integer and bias to unsigned domain [0, 7].\n290\t            int32x4_t q;\n291\t            {\n292\t                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n293\t                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n294\t                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n295\t                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n296\t\n297\t                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n298\t                {\n299\t                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n300\t                }\n301\t            }\n302\t\n303\t            // 4) Split each 3-bit unsigned value into low-2-bit and high-1-bit\n304\t            // halves, packed into one uint16 (low 2 bits per value) plus one\n305\t            // uint8 (high 1 bit per value).\n306\t            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n307\t            uint8_t q1w  = 0;\n308\t            {\n309\t                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n310\t#pragma unroll\n311\t                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n312\t                {\n313\t                    uint32_t v = static_cast<uint32_t>(tw[i]) & 0x7u;\n314\t                    q2w |= static_cast<uint16_t>((v & 0x3u) << (i * 2));\n315\t                    q1w |= static_cast<uint8_t>(((v >> 2) & 0x1u) << i);\n316\t                }\n317\t            }\n318\t\n319\t            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n320\t            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) +          __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n329\t            }\n330\t        }\n331\t    }\n332\t\n333\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n334\t                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n335\t    {\n336\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n337\t        {\n338\t            uint8_t* __builtin_nontemporal_store(q4w, q4w_ptr);\n486\t            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n487\t            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n488\t            {\n489\t recv_buffer,\n495\t                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n496\t    {\n497\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n498\t        {\n499\t            // Directly thread;\n502\t            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n503\t            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n504\t\n505\t            uint32_t q4w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q4w_ptr);\n506\t            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n507\t            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n508\t\n509\t            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n510\t\n511\t            // Unpack q6 into fp16x8_t\n512\t            int32x4_t               static uint constexpr kHalf2_1056 = 0xE420E420; // {-1056.0, -1056.0}, fp16x2_t\n517\t\n518\t#pragma unroll\n519\t                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n520\t                {\n521\t                    int32_t q4 = q4w & kMask000F;\n522\t                    int32_t q2 = (q2w & 0x3) | ((q2w & 0xC) << 14);\n523\t                    q4w >>= 4;\n524\t                    q2w >>= 4;\n525\t                    if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n526\t                    {\n527\t                        int32_t q6 = q4 | (q2 << 4) | kHalf2_1024;\n528\t                        asm volatile(\"v_pk_add_f16 %0, %1, %2\"\n529\t                                     : \"=v\"(w[i])\n530\t                                     : \"v\"(q6), \"v\"(kHalf2_1056));\n531\t                    }\n532\t                    else\n533\t                    {\n534\t                        int32_t int16_2 = q4 | (q2 << 4);\n535\t                        int16_t low     = static_cast<int16_t>(int16_2 & 0xFFFF);\n536\t                        int16_t high    = static_cast<int16_t>((int16_2 >> 16) & 0xFFFF);\n537\t\n538\t                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n539\t                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n540\t                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n541\t                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n542\t                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n543\t                    }\n544\t                }\n545\t            }\n546\t\n547\t            // Apply decoding scales\n548\t            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n549\t            {\n550\t                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n551\t            }\n552\t\n553\t            // That's pretty much it...\n554\t            data[k] = w;\n555\t        }\n556\t    }\n557\t};\n558\t\n559\t// Fp8 symmetric quantization codec.\n560\t// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Fp8 in blocks of 4 *\n561\t// kThreadGroupSize.\n562\ttemplate <typename T, int world_size>\n563\tstruct CodecFP8 : public CodecBase\n564\t{\n565\t    static int constexpr kWorldSize = world_size;\n566\t\n567\t    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n568\t    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n569\t    // into a fp8x8_t (8B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n570\t    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n571\t    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 2176;\n572\t    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 2048;\n573\t    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n574\t    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0, \"kRankTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n575\t\n576\t    static kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n580\t\n581\t    // FP8 Maximum value (on AMD Instinct MI300X - float8_e4m3fnuz)\n582\t    static float constexpr kFP8Max = 240.0f;\n583\t    static int constexpr kScaleFactor =\n584\t        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x1C441C44 : 0x3B883B88; // {1/240.0h, 1/240.0h}\n585\t    static int constexpr kScaleEpsilon =\n586\t        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7; // {1e-7, 1e-7}\n587\t\n588\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecFP8(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n589\t\n590\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n591\t                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n592\t    {\n593\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n594\t        {\n595\t            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n596\t\n597\t            // abs(w)\n598\t            int32x4_t w;\n599\t            {\n600\t                T const* x = reinterpret_cast<T const*>(&atom);\n601\t                T* y       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n602\t                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n603\t                {\n604\t                    y[i] = __habs(x[i]);\n605\t                }\n606\t            }\n607\t\n608\t            // max(w)\n609\t            int wmax;\n610\t            {\n611\t                int a, b;\n612\t                int* dw = reinterpret_cast<int*>(&w);\n613\t                a       = packed_max<T>(dw[0], dw[1]);\n614\t                b       = packed_max<T>(dw[2], dw[3]);\n615\t                wmax    = packed_max<T>(a, b);\n616\t\n617\t                // Reduce the max among a group of 8 threads\n618\t                // Note: This is basically 2 blocks of 32 values setup as the\n619\t                // upper/lower halves of the fp16x2_t\n620\t                for(int i = 1; i < 8; i <<= 1)\n621\t                {\n622\t                    int x = __shfl_down(wmax, i);\n623\t                    wmax  = packed_max<T>(wmax, x);\n624\t                }\n625\t\n626\t                // Share with the cohort\n627\t                wmax = __shfl(wmax, group_leader);\n628\t            }\n629\t\n630\t            // Derive scales\n631\t            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wmax, kScaleFactor);\n632\t            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n633\t            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n634\t\n635\t            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n636\t            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n637\t            {\n638\t                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n639\t            }\n640\t\n641\t            // Convert to packed FP8\n642\t            fp32x8_t wf;\n643\t            {\n644\t                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n645\t                {\n646\t                    half2 const* x = reinterpret_cast<half2 const*>(&w);\n647\t                    float2* y      = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n648\t                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n649\t                    {\n650\t                        y[i] = __half22float2(x[i]);\n651\t                    }\n652\t                }\n653\t                else\n654\t                {\n655\t                    nv_bfloat162 const* x = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162 const*>(&w);\n656\t                    float2* y             = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n657\t                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n658\t                    {\n659\t                        y[i] = __bfloat1622float2(x[i]);\n660\t                    }\n661\t                }\n662\t            }\n663\t\n664\t            int32x2_t qw;\n665\t            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[0], wf[1], qw[0], 0);\n666\t            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[2], wf[3], qw[0], 1);\n667\t            qw[1] =    }\n681\t        }\n682\t    }\n683\t\n684\t    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n685\t                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n686\t    {\n687\t        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n688\t        {\n689\t            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n690\t            uint8_t* atom_ptr __float2bfloat16(val);\n945\t}\n946\t\n947\t// Twoshot QR with an add+RMSNorm epilogue. Unlike the plain QR epilogue,\n948\t// RMSNorm is row-local, so the host launcher only dispatches this variant when\n949\t// each hidden row fits evenly inside one QR tile. For Qwen3.5 hidden_dim=4096\n950\t// bf16 rows, one 32 KiB QR tile contains four independent rows.\n951\ttemplate <typename T, typename CommT, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half = false>\n952\tstruct AllReduceTwoshotRMSNorm\n953\t{\n954\t    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n955\t    static_assert(sizeof(CommT) == 2);\n956\t\n957\t    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n958\t    static constexpr int kElemsPerAtom = sizeof(int32x4_t) / sizeof(T);\n959\t\n960\t    // ======================================================================\n961\t    // TODO(agent): implement the fused two-shot all-reduce + RMSNorm epilogue.\n962\t    //\n963\t    // This kernel must, in ONE pass and without an extra HBM round-trip of the\n964\t    // all-reduced intermediate:\n965\t    //   1. perform the two-shot quick all-reduce of `input` across ranks into a\n966\t    //      register/shared-memory accumulator (see AllReduceTwoshot::run for the\n967\t    //      all-reduce-only version of this exact communication pattern), then\n968\t    //   2. add the per-rank `residual_inp` to the reduced value, writing the sum\n969\t    //      to `residual_out` (the pre-normalization residual stream), then\n970\t    //   3. compute RMSNorm over the `hidden_dim` axis on that sum:\n971\t    //         denom = rsqrt( mean(x^2 over hidden_dim) + eps )\n972\t    //         output = x * denom * weight\n973\t    //      writing the normalized result to `output`.\n974\t    //\n975\t    // `N` = total elements, `hidden_dim` = normalization width, one row per token.\n976\t    // `weight` has `hidden_dim` elements. `T`/`CommT` are fp16 or bf16.\n977\t    //\n978\t    // The current stub only zero-fills the outputs, so it compiles and runs but\n979\t    // does NOT match the reference —               T* __restrict__ output,\n986\t                               T const* __restrict__ weight,\n987\t                               float eps,\n988\t                               uint32_t stream)\n1402\t    {\n1403\t        if(world_size != 2 && world_size != 4 && world_size != 8)\n1404\t        {\n1405\t            throw std::runtime_error(\"All Reduce not supported for world_size = on-device now (see kernel), no host rotation.\n1424\t    }\n1425\t\n1426\t    template <typename T, typename CommT = T, bool cast_bf2half = false>\n1427\t    void allreduce_rmsnorm(T const* A,\n1428\t                           T const* residual_inp,\n1429\t                           T* residual_out,\n1430\t                           T* B,\n1431\t                           T const* weight,\n1432\t                           float eps,\n1433\t                           uint32_t N,\n1434\t                           uint32_t hidden_dim,\n1435\t                           int quant_level,\n1436\t                           hipStream_t stream)\n1437\t    {\n1438\t        if(world_size != 2 && world_size != 4 && world_size != 8)\n1439\t        {\n1440\t            throw std::runtime_error(\"All Reduce Signed range is [-4, +3].\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecQ3 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Layout per quantization block (32 values = 8 threads * 4 fp16x2 lanes):\n    //  - each thread owns 8 values and writes:\n    //      * q2 payload : 8 * 2 bits -> uint16 (2 bytes)\n    //      * q1 payload : 8 * 1 bit  -> uint8  (1 byte)\n    //  - one scale is shared per 32 values and written by group leader.\n    //\n    // kRankTileStride is split as:\n    //   [0   .. 511] : q2 payload region (256 threads * 2 bytes)\n    //   [512 .. 767] : q1 payload region (256 threads * 1 byte)\n    //   [768 .. 895] : scale region (32 groups * 4 bytes)\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 896;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileQ1Offset        = 512;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 768;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // {-1/4.0h, -1/4.0h}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t. encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // 2) Scale + clip to signed int3 range [-4, +3].\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // 4) Split each 3-bit unsigned value into low-2-bit and high-1-bit\n            // halves, packed into one uint16 (low 2 bits per value) plus one\n            // uint8 (high 1 bit per value).\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            uint8_t q1w  = 0;\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    uint32_t v = static_cast<uint32_t>(tw[i]) & reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint8_t* q1w_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ1Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            uint8_t q1w  = *q1w_ptr;\n            int qs }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Fp8 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Fp8 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecFP8 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static int constexpr kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a fp8x8_t (8B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 2176;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 2048;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0, \"kRankTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // FP8 Maximum value (on AMD Instinct MI300X - float8_e4m3fnuz)\n    static float constexpr kFP8Max = 240.0f;\n    static int constexpr kScaleFactor =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x1C441C44 : 0x3B883B88; // {1/240.0h, 1/240.0h}\n    static int constexpr kScaleEpsilon =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7; // {1e-7, 1e-7}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecFP8(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // abs(w)\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                T const* x = reinterpret_cast<T const*>(&atom);\n                T* y       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    y[i] = __habs(x[i]);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // max(w)\n            int wmax;\n            {\n                int a, b;\n                int* dw = reinterpret_cast<int*>(&w);\n                a       = packed_max<T>(dw[0], dw[1]);\n                b       = packed_max<T>(dw[2], dw[3]);\n                wmax    = packed_max<T>(a, b);\n\n                // Reduce the max among a group of 8 threads\n                // Note: This is basically 2 blocks of 32 values setup as the\n                // upper/lower halves of the fp16x2_t\n                for(int i = 1; i < 8; i <<= 1)\n                {\n                    int x = __shfl_down(wmax, i);\n                    wmax  = packed_max<T>(wmax, x);\n                }\n\n                // Share with the cohort\n                wmax = __shfl(wmax, group_leader);\n            }\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n            }\n\n            // Convert to packed FP8\n            fp32x8_t wf;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    half2 const* x = reinterpret_cast<half2 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y      = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __half22float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    nv_bfloat162 const* x = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y             = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __bfloat1622float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            int32x2_t qw;\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[0], wf[1], qw[0], 0);\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[2], wf[3], qw[0], 1);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[4], wf[5], qw[1], 0);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[6], wf[7], qw[1], 1);\n\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            int32x2_t qw = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qw_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack FP8\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 0])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf0[0]), \"v\"(wf0[1]));\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 1])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf1[0]), \"v\"(wf1[1]));\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    __hip_bfloat16* wbf = reinterpret_cast<__hip_bfloat16*>(&w);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 0]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 1]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[1]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 2]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 3]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[1]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Twoshot All Reduce\ntemplate <typename T, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half>\nstruct AllReduceTwoshot\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n\n    __device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                               T* __restrict__ output,\n                               uint32_t const N,                   // number of elements\n                               int const block,                    // block index\n                               int const rank,                     // rank index\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list, // communication buffers\n                               uint32_t const data_offset, // offset to start of the data buffer\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        // Topology\n        int thread           = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n        uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n        Codec codec(thread, rank);\n        int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n        uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n        for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        {\n            buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Read input into registers\n        int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                    half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1A: Write segment data into the communication buffer of the target\n        // rank responsible for this segment.\n        uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n        uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n\n        uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1B: Reduce the segment data from the communication buffers.\n        int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // note: we reuse tA as temp buffer here\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                {\n                    packed_assign_add<T>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Write the reduced segment to every other rank\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags1_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Read the gather segments from the rank's communication buffer.\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data1_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags1_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // Gather all reduced and final rank segments into tA.\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Write the result to output.\n        BufferResource dst_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t dst_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n                nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                    bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n                }\n                buffer_store_dwordx4(*reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf),\n                                     dst_buffer.descriptor,\n                                     dst_offset,\n                                     0,\n                                     0);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                buffer_store_dwordx4(tA[i], dst_buffer.descriptor, dst_offset, 0, 0);\n            }\n            dst_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\ntemplate <typename T>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float(T val);\n\ntemplate <>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float<half>(half val)\n{\n    return __half2float(val);\n}\n\ntemplate <>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float<__hip_bfloat16>(__hip_bfloat16 __float2bfloat16(val);\n}\n\n// Twoshot QR with an add+RMSNorm epilogue. AllReduceTwoshotRMSNorm\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n    static_assert(sizeof(CommT) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kElemsPerAtom = sizeof(int32x4_t) / sizeof(T);\n\n    // ======================================================================\n    // TODO(agent): implement the fused two-shot all-reduce + RMSNorm epilogue.\n    //\n    // This kernel must, in ONE pass and without an extra HBM round-trip of the\n    // all-reduced intermediate:\n    //   1. perform the two-shot quick all-reduce of `input` across ranks into a\n    //      register/shared-memory accumulator (see AllReduceTwoshot::run for the\n    //      all-reduce-only version of this exact communication pattern), then\n    //   2. add With hidden_dim >= 128 (bf16),\n        // rows_per_tile <= 128, so 512 bytes. Very small.\n\n        // But we need to reduce across all threads that contribute to the same row.\n        // Strategy: each thread computes partial sum of squares for each row it touches,\n        // then we do a wavefront reduction + shared memory reduction.\n\n        // Compute per-row partial sum of x^2 for this thread\n        // We'll store partial sums in shared mem indexed by row.\n        extern __shared__ char smem_raw[];\n        float* smem_row_ss = reinterpret_cast<float*>(smem_raw);\n        // smem layout: rows_per_tile floats for the partial sums\n\n        // Initialize shared memory\n        for(uint32_t r = thread; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                    bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n                }\n                ar_atom = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                ar_atom = tA[i];\n            }\n\n            // Add residual in T precision, store to x_vals as float\n            T* ar_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&ar_atom);\n            T* res_ptr = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&res_atom);\n            T x_T[kEPA];\n#pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < kEPA; j++)\n            {\n                float ar_f  = qr_to_float<T>(ar_ptr[j]);\n                float res_f = qr_to_float<T>(res_ptr[j]);\n                float sum   = ar_f + res_f;\n                x_vals[i * kEPA + j] = sum;\n                x_T[j] = qr_from_float<T>(sum);\n            }\n\n            // Write residual_out\n            int32x4_t out_atom = *reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(x_T);\n            BufferResource res_out_buffer(residual_out, N * sizeof(T));\n            uint32_t res_out_off = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t) + i * kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            buffer_store_dwordx4(out_atom, res_out_buffer.descriptor, res_out_off, 0, 0);\n        }\n\n        // Now compute RMSNorm per row.\n        // Each thread's elements are strided: for atom i, element j, the global\n        // element index within the tile is: thread * kEPA + i * kAtomStride * kEPA + j\n        // = thread * 8 + i * 256 * 8 + j = thread * 8 + i * 2048 + j\n        // The row index for a given element = (tile_elem_start + elem_in_tile) / hidden_dim\n        // The position within the row = (tile_elem_start + elem_in_tile) % hidden_dim\n\n        // Use shared memory for per-row partial sums of squares\n        // Max rows per tile: kElemsPerTile / hidden_dim. For hidden_dim=4096, bf16:\n        // kElemsPerTile = 32768/2 = 16384, rows_per_tile = 4.\n        // For hidden_dim=128, rows_per_tile = 128. Max is kElemsPerTile (hidden_dim=1 not realistic).\n        // We'll use a reasonable upper bound. Since hidden_dim * sizeof(T) divides kTileSize,\n        // rows_per_tile = kTileSize / (hidden_dim * sizeof(T)).\n        // Max shared mem = rows_per_tile * sizeof(float). With hidden_dim >= 128 (bf16),\n        // rows_per_tile <= 128, so 512 bytes. Very small.\n\n        // But we need to reduce across all threads that contribute to the same row.\n        // Strategy: each thread computes partial sum of squares for each row it touches,\n        // then we do a wavefront reduction + shared memory reduction.\n\n        // Compute per-row partial sum of x^2 for this thread\n        // We'll store partial sums in shared mem indexed by row.\n        extern __shared__ char smem_raw[];\n        float* smem_row_ss = reinterpret_cast<float*>(smem_raw);\n        // smem layout: rows_per_tile floats for the partial sums\n\n        // Initialize shared memory\n        for(uint32_t r = thread; r < rows_per_tile; r += kBlockSize)\n        {\n            smem_row_ss[r] = 0.0f;\n        }\n        __syncthreads();\n\n        // Each thread computes partial sums per row and atomically adds to shared mem\n        // Element layout in tile for thread t, atom i, sub-element j:\n        //   elem_in_tile = i * (kAtomStride * kEPA) + t * kEPA + j\n        //                = i * 2048 + t * 8 + j  (for kAtomStride=256, kEPA=8)\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            uint32_t base_elem = i * (kAtomStride * kEPA) + thread * kEPA;\n            for(int j = 0; j < kEPA; j++)\n            {\n                uint32_t elem_in_tile = base_elem + j;\n                uint32_t row_in_tile  = elem_in_tile / hidden_dim;\n                float val = x_vals[i * kEPA + j];\n                atomicAdd(&smem_row_ss[row_in_tile], val * val);\n            }\n        }\n        __syncthreads();\n\n        // Compute rsqrt(mean(x^2) + eps) for each row, store back in smem\n        for(uint32_t r = thread; r < rows_per_tile; r += kBlockSize)\n        {\n            float mean_sq = smem_row_ss[r] / (float)hidden_dim;\n            smem_row_ss[r] = rsqrtf(mean_sq + eps);\n        }\n        __syncthreads();\n\n        // Load weight into registers or access from global memory\n        // Apply RMSNorm: output = x * denom * weight and write to output\n        BufferResource wt_buffer(const_cast<T*>(weight), hidden_dim * sizeof(T));\n        BufferResource out_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            uint32_t base_elem = i * (kAtomStride * kEPA) + thread * kEPA;\n            T out_vals[kEPA];\n#pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < kEPA; j++)\n            {\n                uint32_t elem_in_tile = base_elem + j;\n                uint32_t row_in_tile  = elem_in_tile / hidden_dim;\n                uint32_t col          = elem_in_tile % hidden_dim;\n\n                float denom = smem_row_ss[row_in_tile];\n                float val   = x_vals[i * kEPA + j];\n\n                // Load weight for this column\n                uint32_t wt_byte_offset = col * sizeof(T);\n                // Use scalar load for weight\n                T* wt_ptr  = const_cast<T*>(weight) + col;\n                float w_f  = qr_to_float<T>(*wt_ptr);\n\n                float normed = val * denom * w_f;\n                out_vals[j]  = qr_from_float<T>(normed);\n            }\n\n            int32x4_t out_atom = *reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(out_vals);\n            uint32_t out_off = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t) + i * kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            buffer_store_dwordx4(out_atom, out_buffer.descriptor, out_off, 0, 0);\n        }\n    }","originalFile":"#pragma once\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT\n// Copyright (C) 2024-2026, Advanced Micro Devices, Inc. fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMin = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xD000D000 : 0xC200C200;\n\n    // {+31, +31}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMax = std::is_same<T, half>::value rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // Compute the absolute maximum of the atom in the thread group\n            // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale;\n            int encoding_scale;\n            decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // Convert from f16x2_t to uint16x2_t\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Pack 8 x q6 into int32_t + int16_t\n            uint32_t q4w;\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            q4w = (q[0] & 0x000F000F) | ((q[1] & 0x000F000F) << 4) | ((q[2] & 0x000F000F) << 8) |\n                  ((q[3] & 0x000F000F) << 12);\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    q2w |= (tw[i] >> 4) << (i * 2);\n                }\n            }\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q4w, q4w_ptr);\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint32_t q4w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q4w_ptr);\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack q6 into fp16x8_t\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                static uint constexpr kMask000F   = 0x000F000F;\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1024 = 0x64006400; // {1024.0, 1024.0}, fp16x2_t\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1056 = 0xE420E420; // {-1056.0, -1056.0}, fp16x2_t\n\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    int32_t q4 = q4w & kMask000F;\n                    int32_t q2 = (q2w & 0x3) | ((q2w & 0xC) << 14);\n                    q4w >>= 4;\n                    q2w >>= 4;\n                    if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                    {\n                        int32_t q6 = q4 | (q2 << 4) | kHalf2_1024;\n                        asm volatile(\"v_pk_add_f16 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i])\n                                     : \"v\"(q6), \"v\"(kHalf2_1056));\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        int32_t int16_2 = q4 | (q2 << 4);\n                        int16_t low     = static_cast<int16_t>(int16_2 & 0xFFFF);\n                        int16_t high    = static_cast<int16_t>((int16_2 >> 16) & 0xFFFF);\n\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Fp8 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Fp8 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecFP8 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static int constexpr kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a fp8x8_t (8B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 2176;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 2048;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0, \"kRankTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // FP8 Maximum value (on AMD Instinct MI300X - float8_e4m3fnuz)\n    static float constexpr kFP8Max = 240.0f;\n    static int constexpr kScaleFactor =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x1C441C44 : 0x3B883B88; // {1/240.0h, 1/240.0h}\n    static int constexpr kScaleEpsilon =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7; // {1e-7, 1e-7}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecFP8(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // abs(w)\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                T const* x = reinterpret_cast<T const*>(&atom);\n                T* y       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    y[i] = __habs(x[i]);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // max(w)\n            int wmax;\n            {\n                int a, b;\n                int* dw = reinterpret_cast<int*>(&w);\n                a       = packed_max<T>(dw[0], dw[1]);\n                b       = packed_max<T>(dw[2], dw[3]);\n                wmax    = packed_max<T>(a, b);\n\n                // Reduce the max among a group of 8 threads\n                // Note: This is basically 2 blocks of 32 values setup as the\n                // upper/lower halves of the fp16x2_t\n                for(int i = 1; i < 8; i <<= 1)\n                {\n                    int x = __shfl_down(wmax, i);\n                    wmax  = packed_max<T>(wmax, x);\n                }\n\n                // Share with the cohort\n                wmax = __shfl(wmax, group_leader);\n            }\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n            }\n\n            // Convert to packed FP8\n            fp32x8_t wf;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    half2 const* x = reinterpret_cast<half2 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y      = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __half22float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    nv_bfloat162 const* x = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y             = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __bfloat1622float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            int32x2_t qw;\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[0], wf[1], qw[0], 0);\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[2], wf[3], qw[0], 1);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[4], wf[5], qw[1], 0);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[6], wf[7], qw[1], 1);\n\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            int32x2_t qw = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qw_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack FP8\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 0])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf0[0]), \"v\"(wf0[1]));\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 1])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf1[0]), \"v\"(wf1[1]));\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    __hip_bfloat16* wbf = reinterpret_cast<__hip_bfloat16*>(&w);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 1]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[1]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 2]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[0]);\n <typename T, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half>\nstruct AllReduceTwoshot\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n\n    __device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                               T* __restrict__ output,\n                               uint32_t const N,                   // number of elements\n                               int const block,                    // block index\n                               int const rank,                     // rank index\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list, // communication buffers\n                               uint32_t const data_offset, // offset to start of the data buffer\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        // Topology\n        int thread           = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n        uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n        Codec codec(thread, rank);\n        int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n        uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n        for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        {\n            buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Read input into registers\n        int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1A: Write segment data into the communication buffer of the target\n        // rank responsible for this segment.\n        uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n        uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n\n        uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset +   int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1B: Reduce the segment data from the communication buffers.\n        int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // note: we reuse tA as temp buffer here\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                {\n                    packed_assign_add<T>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Write the reduced segment to every other rank\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags1_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Read the gather segments from the rank's communication buffer.\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data1_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags1_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // Gather all reduced and final rank segments into tA.\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Write the result to output.\n        BufferResource dst_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t dst_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n                nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                    bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n                }\n                buffer_store_dwordx4(*reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf),\n                                     dst_buffer.descriptor,\n                                     dst_offset,\n                                     0,\n                                     0);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                buffer_store_dwordx4(tA[i], dst_buffer.descriptor, dst_offset, 0, 0);\n            }\n            dst_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\ntemplate <typename T>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float(T val);\n\ntemplate <>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float<half>(half val)\n{\n    return __half2float(val);\n}\n\ntemplate <>\n__quickreduce_device_inline__ float qr_to_float<__hip_bfloat16>(__hip_bfloat16 __float2bfloat16(val);\n}\n\n// Twoshot QR with an add+RMSNorm epilogue. AllReduceTwoshotRMSNorm\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n    static_assert(sizeof(CommT) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kElemsPerAtom = sizeof(int32x4_t) / sizeof(T);\n\n    // ======================================================================\n    // TODO(agent): implement the fused two-shot all-reduce + RMSNorm epilogue.\n    //\n    // This kernel must, in ONE pass and without an extra HBM round-trip of the\n    // all-reduced intermediate:\n    //   1. perform the two-shot quick all-reduce of `input` across ranks into a\n    //      register/shared-memory accumulator (see AllReduceTwoshot::run for the\n    //      all-reduce-only version of this exact communication pattern), then\n    //   2. add the per-rank `residual_inp` to the reduced value, writing the sum\n    //      to `residual_out` (the pre-normalization residual stream), then\n    //   3. compute RMSNorm over the `hidden_dim` axis on that sum:\n    //         denom = rsqrt( mean(x^2 over hidden_dim) + eps )\n    //         output = x * denom * weight\n    //      writing the normalized result to `output`.\n    //\n    // `N` =                          float eps,\n                               uint32_t const N,\n                               uint32_t const hidden_dim,\n                               int const block,\n                               int const rank,\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list,\n                               uint32_t const data_offset,\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        // Stub: zero the outputs for this block's tile so the kernel is a no-op\n        // placeholder. blockDim.x * blockDim.y + thread;\n            idx < N;\n            idx += (uint32_t)grid * blockDim.x * blockDim.y)\n        {\n            output[idx]       = qr_from_float<T>(0.0f);\n            residual_out[idx] = qr_from_float<T>(0.0f);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n\n// from quickreduce.h\n#define HIP_CHECK(err)                                                                             \\\n
